< review>
I stayed here for 5 nights. Two of those nights I got two different rooms. Each room had one bed. The shower and bathroom was ok. The shower is bit small for me. I am a big guy. Each room was a bit different, bud the decor and interior design of each was nice. Each feature a big clock, a flat screen tv,  refrigerator. Only one of the rooms I was in had a microwave. I would have given 5 stars. But two of the rooms power outlets needed fixing, and its clear that some of the rooms are in need of repair. Overall great value for the price, as la has notoriously high room rates. Thanks for a great place to stay.<//review>

<Time>1551919159560</Time><Rating>4</Rating>< Text>
The room was clean and the price is right for how close it is too the beach, this place is all about location, an easy 5 minute walk or less to the beach. Santa Monica pier isn't much farther as well as numerous restaurants, parks and activities. It does have an older feel and could use some updates but I love the open air concept and the patio looks like an awesome spot to hang out if it wasn't raining on us the whole time. It is right on Ocean Ave so traffic can be heard almost constantly and parking is limited but we had no problem getting a spot and keeping it for the 2 days we were here.
Again as far as price and location go, I'd definitely stay here again.< /Text>

<userid>106786523448580698569< /userid>< name>
Sara Clawson</name>
<date>1553777679468< /date><Rate>4</Rate>< review>
My fiance and I took a spontaneous trip to Santa Monica in November 2018. We were trying to find the cheapest hotel near the beach/pier when we came across this little hidden gem. Here are the pros and cons:

Pros
Amazing location
Friendly staff
Fresh towels
Cleanliness
Price (cheapest in the area)
20 minutes from LAX and the LA area

Cons
No A/C
No shampoo, body wash, etc. provided
First come first serve parking with tiny spaces
The water pressure is VERY hit or miss and adjusting the temperature is a little difficult.

Overall, though, the experience was great. And for the price, you won't find anything better. I highly recommend staying here and I will definitely be back in the future.</review>

<rating>1< /rating>< review>
We chose Seaview because of it's location,  plus we were in a tight budget, also we're not from California so we didn't know about other affordable hotels that were very good & near Santa Monica beach. We stayed for 3 nights & it wasn't pleasant. I did like that the rooms were not visible like right on the main street; however this hotel is in major need of repairs. Our room's heater was not working and it was pretty cold -about upper 30's -40 degrees (nightime) when we visited. We had to let the water run for a good 20 min. so that we could finally get some hot water and while taking a shower the water would not level out to warm. So it was either too hot or cold. Tub is very old/small. Everything outside our door, on top of our room and wall to wall can be heard in the room. The room did have a sink, microwave, refrigerator, tv and an extension cord. Beds were below average-and there were stains on bedding sheets; even though the bedding smelled washed. For the price we paid for the 3 nights- we expected better since we did pay a whole lot more than $88/night. The room had a window sliding door to let you walk out into your small private outdoor area with table & chair; which was nice BUT at nighttime it felt unsafe since we could not lock it and there was also a small window in the bathroom that could not be locked either. I feel that the hotel needs to make the necessary repairs/ renovations & safety measures to accommodate guests better. Starting with the heating & plumbing. I could not & wouldn't want to imagine being in this hotel during the summer without any A.C. The pro's is that everyday the room was cleaned and they did leave behind soaps & toilet paper. Also the rooftop was nice -although it could be better. The hotel is very close to muscle beach & Santa Monica beach/pier. On my next visit to Santa Monica, I I will definitely pay the same or a tad bit more to stay elsewhere -given that now I know of other good, safe affordable hotels nearby. I chose this hotel over others based on the good reviews, and I made a mistake in doing so. I must say that our room did not look like the pictures. Next time I'll do major research! Overall, this hotel is in dire need of necessary repairs/ renovations & safety measures!< /review>

<Text>Affordable hotel for the area.  A hotel next door and across the street would be 3 times the cost.  When you first check in you will be asked if you want to look at the room and verify that you want to stay.  You will be charged the total amount for your stay upfront.  Prices are cheaper if you pay with cash.  There is free parking.  A walk down the alley will take you to the beach in a couple of minutes.  There is alot of restaurants and shops within walking distance. I had a rental car but barely used it.  There is an outdoor patio area which is nice in the evening to hang out.  The room i stayed in had a kitchen with microwave, stovetop, and fridge.  The bathroom does not have a bathtub only a shower.  There is no air conditioner but being by the ocean it is not really needed on most days.  An oscillating fan is provided.  There is cable tv and free wifi.  Keeping the cost in mind compared to the surrounding hotels, it is not the best.  It is adequate.  The bed isn't the most comfortable but it is a king size.  I had a room near the street and it can get loud.  I had to close the windows and shut the doors to the bathroom and kitchen to keep the noise out.  The door only has a lock on the knob but they do have security cameras around.  You get what you pay for but i enjoyed staying in the area with the beach being close by.  You're not going to spend much time in your room anyway with so much to do near by.  If you want a nicer room and still stay in the area, you will pay 3-4 times more.< /Text><Time>1506464499324</Time><name>Jericho Datu</name></record></dataset><record>

< review>
The bus didn't pick us up that morning.  Instead we were picked up by a nice guy in a van, driven one hour to SF to pick up another couple then driven to meet the bus in Oakland Chinatown.  The lady tour guide checked us in without saying hello or introduced herself and the bus driver nicely so we could remember their names.  You spent a lot of time on the bus and when the bus stopped we were rushed like schoolchildren on field trips.  The tour guide didn't pronounce location names correctly and she treated us like we were all dumb.  She was outright rude and mean sometimes, she must know most Asian customers rarely complain.  On second day we had to rush through lunch to buy stuff for dinner because she told us there were no restaurants near our hotel that night.  When we almost got there she told us there are actually some restaurants within 10-15 minutes walk. The manager at the Days Inn in Klamath Falls were very nice at the breakfast buffet.  On the way back to drop us off, the driver ran into some dangerous looking dead end corner where some homeless guys could have thrown things at our bus.  This trip was more suitable for people who speak little English and have little knowledge of the US.  We had been on other tours before and know the differences.  We are not dumb but we gave the guide tips anyway because we are decent people while she asked for tips without showing grace or gratitude.</review>

<Text>47 Hill Brewing Company was a very nice Brewery. It was very clean and had a nice atmosphere. We showed up a little later in the night and the place was packed. Even with it being packed service was overall all very decent servers seemed a bit rushed so in turn not all that friendly but that could be expected with how busy it was.

Beers were very good and the food looked and smelled amazing but we had already eaten so we didn't get a chance to try any.

Not being from around the area the only main issue was getting to the brewery especially in the dark. It was hard to know where to turn as the street side of the building is not well lit and didnt see signs we had to do a couple u turns to finally get into the back parking lot where the main entrance is and that side of the building is all well lit.

The outdoor space is very nice and there is plenty of space inside and outside of the brewery for big groups.

I would definitely recommend this brewery to anyone looking at breweries in the area.< /Text><Gmap_id>0x808f79b9ef28740b:0x1abd079d7d33a9c5<//Gmap_id></record></dataset><record>

< review>
I came here to meet a few friends for lunch. A few of my friends had been there already, saying a flight was only $15. The brewery was hidden behind some buildings, and the entrance was also in the back. They had a small parking lot in the back. There was some outdoor benches to sit at. We walked in and I immediately noticed how big it was inside. It seemed big, but actually not that many benches/tables to sit at. They also allowed dogs inside. After sitting down, they had some pinball/arcade machines on the side. There were a few board games also.

I was pretty set on getting a flight since it was cheap, but then I noticed how small their selection was. They offer 20oz and 10oz cups. I ended up trying and getting the Pink Boots IPA. It wasn't as bitter as most IPA's and I really liked it. I also ordered a chicken quesadilla. My friends got the cider, wings, and the steak sandwich. The food came out pretty fast after we ordered. The quesadilla was average sized and came with sour cream, salsa, and guac. The steak sandwich looked really good and came with fries. The wings were spicy. The food went well with our drinks.

Overall, the brewery is nice with a parking lot, open space, and games. I wish they had some more drink options. I would probably come back again since it's convenient and affordable.</review>

<review>What a fun place to relax.  Grab a beer & head  outside for bench & table.  The Decoy reminds of  kolsch I've tasted in Munich.  This was refreshing & light, a nice way to start the evening.  Ordered the Bavarian bratwurst with all the fixings.  Not sure but the veggies tasted as if it may have been steamed in beer; which wouldn't be surprising.  The brat has a kick along with the lovely aromatic herbs.  Excellent!  The poutine has (beer!) gravy, medium cheddar, flecks of beef, & scallions.  The fries were sized between a steak frite and a shoestring.  They were a bit aggressive on the gravy, bottom resulted soggy fries.  Whomp whomp.  Well, unless that's your thing!   If you like hoppy beer, the Slappy IPA may be your drink.  Heady, bold, nice finish.  Stands on its own - I really like it!  The meatballs & garlic bread was filling and fulfilling. < review>
Great new brewery in town.   They have parking in back or easy on street parking.

Once you walk in note the high ceilings with open atmosphere.  They have a long bar, long tables, and an outdoor patio.   A couple tvs hang up high on the walls so great for watching games.

They had about 5 beers on tap ranging from light to a dark porter.  You can do a sampler or just get a pint of whatever you like.

Starting 5/13 they will open the kitchen and start serving small bites.  Yum.< /review>

< review>
I've taken two of my dogs there and seen both ends of the spectrum: compassion when treating and eventually euthanizing my first one and excitement when performing a wellness check with my new puppy.

When planning to say goodbye to our last dog, they were patient and understanding while we decided, and NEVER came across as cold or impatient. In fact, I could see the doctor's eyes swell with tears as my wife and I cried while we put him down. While treating our new puppy Dr Evans is absolutely fantastic with him. The best way to describe it is that it's like he's treating his own pet - how can you ask for more?  I wish family doctors had that type of communication skills. I get appointments relatively promptly and have not had to wait long when arriving.

My only suggestion for improvement is the clinic doesn't feel or smell as clean as other vets I've used, but in no way will that deter me from staying with them.<//review>

It only eased the pain for a bit but, when the effect of the medication was gone, my back ache flared up. I was hurting so much, I couldn't stand the pain one more day. I started to search for a Chiropractor online and  I came across Dr. Cheung. I phoned his office, I explained my situation to  the receptionist whom, was very helpful and scheduled me a same day appoitnment. I can tell that I felt better, I was able to walk with less pain. Within the past week, I have been to his office 3 times and already feel much much better. I would definitely recommend his services.
